      ],
      "source": [
        "import osos\n",
        "import shutil\n",
        "import sys\n",
        "from pathlib import Path\n",
        "from nerfstudio.process_data.colmap_utils import colmap_to_json\n",
        "\n",
        "# ================= CONFIGURATION =================\n",
        "project_name = \"car_scan\"\n",
        "original_video_path = '/content/drive/MyDrive/3DLAB/video_car.mp4'\n",
        "\n",
        "output_dir = f\"/content/{project_name}\"\n",
        "database_path = f\"{output_dir}/database.db\"\n",
        "images_dir = f\"{output_dir}/images\"\n",
        "sparse_path = f\"{output_dir}/sparse\"\n",
        "# =================================================\n",
        "\n",
        "# 1. Clean previous run\n",
        "if os.path.exists(output_dir):\n",
        "    shutil.rmtree(output_dir)\n",
        "os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n",
        "os.makedirs(images_dir, exist_ok=True)\n",
        "\n",
        "# 2. Downscale Video (เปลี่ยนเป็นลดแค่ 2 เท่า เพื่อให้ภาพชัดขึ้น COLMAP จะได้หาจุดง่ายขึ้น)\n",
        "downscaled_video_path = f'/content/{project_name}_downscaled.mp4'\n",
        "print(f\"1️⃣ Downscaling video (High Res)...\")\n",
        "# scale='iw/2:ih/2' = ลดขนาดแค่ครึ่งเดียว\n",
        "!ffmpeg -y -i \"{original_video_path}\" -vf scale='iw/2:ih/2' -c:v libx264 -preset medium -crf 23 -c:a copy \"{downscaled_video_path}\" > /dev/null 2>&1\n",
        "\n",
        "# 3. Extract Frames (fps=5 พอดีๆ ไม่เยอะไม่น้อยเกินไป)\n",
        "print(f\"2️⃣ Extracting frames...\")\n",
        "!ffmpeg -y -i \"{downscaled_video_path}\" -vf \"fps=5\" \"{images_dir}/frame_%05d.png\" -hide_banner -loglevel error\n",
        "\n",
        "num_images = len(os.listdir(images_dir))\n",
        "print(f\"✅ Extracted {num_images} images.\")\n",
        "\n",
        "# 4. Feature Extraction (CPU)\n",
        "print(f\"3️⃣ Running Feature Extraction (CPU)...\")\n",
        "if os.path.exists(database_path):\n",
        "    os.remove(database_path)\n",
        "\n",
        "cmd_extract = [\n",
        "    \"colmap\", \"feature_extractor\",\n",
        "    \"--database_path\", database_path,\n",
        "    \"--image_path\", images_dir,\n",
        "    \"--ImageReader.camera_model\", \"OPENCV\",\n",
        "    \"--SiftExtraction.use_gpu\", \"0\",\n",
        "    \"--SiftExtraction.num_threads\", \"16\"\n",
        "]\n",
        "!{\" \".join(cmd_extract)}\n",
        "\n",
        "# 5. Matching (Sequential - เร็วกว่า Exhaustive มาก)\n",
        "print(f\"4️⃣ Running Matching (Sequential - Optimized)...\")\n",
        "# ใช้ SequentialMatcher เหมาะกับวิดีโอ และเร็วกว่ามาก\n",
        "cmd_match = [\n",
        "    \"colmap\", \"sequential_matcher\",\n",
        "    \"--database_path\", database_path,\n",
        "    \"--SiftMatching.use_gpu\", \"0\",\n",
        "    \"--SequentialMatching.loop_detection\", \"1\", # ช่วยหาจุดวนกลับมาที่เดิม\n",
        "    \"--SequentialMatching.overlap\", \"20\"        # ให้เปรียบเทียบ 20 ภาพใกล้เคียง (เพิ่มโอกาสเจอคู่ภาพ)\n",
        "]\n",
        "!{\" \".join(cmd_match)}\n",
        "\n",
        "# 6. Mapper\n",
        "print(f\"5️⃣ Running Mapper...\")\n",
        "os.makedirs(sparse_path, exist_ok=True)\n",
        "cmd_mapper = [\n",
        "    \"colmap\", \"mapper\",\n",
        "    \"--database_path\", database_path,\n",
        "    \"--image_path\", images_dir,\n",
        "    \"--output_path\", sparse_path,\n",
        "    \"--Mapper.init_min_tri_angle\", \"4\",\n",
        "    \"--Mapper.multiple_models\", \"0\" # บังคับให้สร้างโมเดลเดียว\n",
        "]\n",
        "!{\" \".join(cmd_mapper)}\n",
        "\n",
        "# 7. Convert to transforms.json (แก้ Error ตรงนี้แล้ว)\n",
        "print(f\"6️⃣ Generating transforms.json...\")\n",
        "recon_dir = Path(f\"{sparse_path}/0\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if not recon_dir.exists():\n",
        "    print(\"❌ ERROR: COLMAP failed again.\")\n",
        "    print(\"สรุป: วิดีโอนี้น่าจะ 'ยากเกินไป' สำหรับ COLMAP ครับ (รถเงาเกินไป/ไม่มีลวดลาย)\")\n",
        "else:\n",
        "    # 🔴 แก้ไข: ลบ argument ที่ไม่จำเป็นออก เพื่อแก้ TypeError\n",
        "    colmap_to_json(\n",
        "        recon_dir=recon_dir,\n",
        "        output_dir=Path(output_dir),\n",
        "    )\n",
        "\n",
        "    if os.path.exists(f\"{output_dir}/transforms.json\"):\n",
        "        print(f\"✅ SUCCESS! transforms.json created at: {output_dir}/transforms.json\")\n",
        "        print(\"🚀 Ready for Training (Cell 4)!\")\n",
        "    else:\n",
        "        print(\"❌ Error converting to transforms.json\")"
      ]
    },

        "import os\n",
        "\n",
        "# กำหนดโฟลเดอร์ต้นทาง (ใน Colab) และปลายทาง (ใน Google Drive)\n",
        "source_dir = \"/content/car_scan\"\n",
        "destination_dir = \"/content/drive/MyDrive/3DLAB/car_scan_backup\"\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"📦 กำลังสำรองข้อมูลจาก {source_dir} ไปยัง {destination_dir} ...\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if os.path.exists(source_dir):\n",
        "    # ลบ Backup เก่าถ้ามี (เพื่อให้ได้ไฟล์ล่าสุดเสมอ)\n",
        "    if os.path.exists(destination_dir):\n",

        "## 5. Export and Save\n",
        "Export to `.splat` and save to Google Drive."
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "execution_count": null,
      "metadata": {
        "colab": {
          "background_save": true
        },
        "id": "rQlLKQHSnQG3"
      },
      "outputs": [],
      "source": [
        "import os\n",
        "import glob\n",
        "import shutil\n",
        "from pathlib import Path\n",
        "\n",
        "# ================= CONFIGURATION =================\n",
        "project_name = \"car_scan\"\n",
        "# โฟลเดอร์ที่เก็บผลการเทรน (ใน Colab)\n",
        "training_output_dir = Path(f\"outputs/{project_name}/splatfacto\")\n",
        "# โฟลเดอร์ปลายทางที่จะเซฟงานจบ (ใน Google Drive)\n",
        "drive_output_dir = Path(\"/content/drive/MyDrive/3DLAB\")\n",
        "# =================================================\n",
        "\n",
        "print(f\"🔍 กำลังค้นหาไฟล์ Config ล่าสุดใน: {training_output_dir}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "if not training_output_dir.exists():\n",
        "    print(f\"❌ Error: ไม่พบโฟลเดอร์ผลลัพธ์ ({training_output_dir})\")\n",
        "    print(\"👉 คุณรัน Cell 4 (Training) เสร็จสมบูรณ์หรือยังครับ?\")\n",
        "else:\n",
        "    # หาโฟลเดอร์ย่อยทั้งหมด (แต่ละโฟลเดอร์คือการเทรน 1 ครั้ง)\n",
        "    # ใช้ os.scandir เพื่อประสิทธิภาพที่ดีกว่า (ลด system calls)\n",
        "    latest_run = None\n",
        "    latest_time = -1\n",
        "\n",
        "    if training_output_dir.exists():\n",
        "        try:\n",
        "            with os.scandir(training_output_dir) as entries:\n",
        "                for entry in entries:\n",
        "                    if entry.is_dir():\n",
        "                        mtime = entry.stat().st_mtime\n",
        "                        if mtime > latest_time:\n",
        "                            latest_time = mtime\n",
        "                            latest_run = Path(entry.path)\n",
        "        except OSError:\n",
        "            pass\n",
        "\n",
        "    if not latest_run:\n",
        "        print(\"❌ Error: ไม่พบประวัติการเทรนเลย\")\n",
        "    else:\n",
        "        # เลือกโฟลเดอร์ที่เวลาใหม่ที่สุด (Latest Run)\n",
        "        config_path = latest_run / \"config.yml\"\n",
        "\n",
        "        if not config_path.exists():\n",
        "             print(f\"❌ Error: ไม่พบไฟล์ config.yml ใน {latest_run}\")\n",
        "        else:\n",
        "            print(f\"✅ พบ Config ล่าสุดที่: {config_path}\")\n",
        "\n",
        "            # --- 1. เริ่มกระบวนการ Export ---\n",
        "            print(\"🚀 กำลังแปลงไฟล์โมเดลเป็น .splat ...\")\n",
        "            # คำสั่ง Export ของ Nerfstudio\n",
        "            !ns-export gaussian-splat --load-config \"{config_path}\" --output-dir \"{latest_run}\"\n",
        "\n",
        "            # --- 2. ย้ายไฟล์เข้า Google Drive ---\n",
        "            # หาไฟล์ .splat ที่เพิ่งสร้างเสร็จ\n",
        "            generated_splats = list(latest_run.glob(\"*.splat\"))\n",
        "\n",
        "            if generated_splats:\n",
        "                source_splat = generated_splats[0]\n",
        "                # ตั้งชื่อไฟล์ปลายทาง\n",
        "                dest_splat = drive_output_dir / f\"{project_name}_final.splat\"\n",
        "\n",
        "                # สร้างโฟลเดอร์ใน Drive เผื่อยังไม่มี\n",
        "                drive_output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n",
        "\n",
        "                print(f\"💾 กำลังบันทึกไฟล์ลง Google Drive: {dest_splat}\")\n",
        "                shutil.copy(source_splat, dest_splat)\n",
        "                print(\"-\" * 50)\n",
        "                print(f\"🎉 เสร็จสมบูรณ์! ไฟล์งานของคุณอยู่ที่: Google Drive > 3DLAB > {project_name}_final.splat\")\n",
        "                print(\"คุณสามารถดาวน์โหลดไฟล์นี้ไปเปิดดูในเว็บ https://gsplat.tech/ หรือ https://poly.cam/tools/gaussian-splatting ได้เลยครับ\")\n",
        "                print(\"-\" * 50)\n",
        "            else:\n",
        "                print(\"❌ Error: คำสั่ง Export ทำงานเสร็จ แต่ไม่พบไฟล์ .splat (ลองเช็ค Log ด้านบน)\")"
      ]
    }
